                      <div data-reactid="1132">
                       The high ceiling-loft style apartment, makes you feel like your living in New York City with all the joys of sunny California right outside. Enjoy a gourmet kitchen, roof access to the pool and hot tub, and a variety of bars/restaurants minutes away! Beautiful large DOWNTOWN Los Angeles 1 bedroom, 850 sq ft loft. Lots of natural light and located on Spring Street making it the perfect location and close proximity of many things!! AMENITIES: new wood floors, modern stainless steel and granite kitchen, exposed concrete beams, high ~11ft ceilings. 1-bedroom, full bathroom and large living and dining area. Also has a rooftop pool and gym. BATHROOM: has a large tub, hair Dryer and towels included. BEDROOM: comes with 22" TV, Smart DVD player, which includes Netflix, and a Super Nintendo game consol (Mario &amp; Donkey Kong games), California queen-size bed and extremely comfortable mattress. LIVING ROOM: 55" Smart HDTV with Netflix, Hulu+ and Pandora. Has modern furniture with an extremely comfortable sectional sofa that could sleep 2 additional people. Beautiful paintings and art on the wall, which gives it a more “homey” feel. KITCHEN: modern stainless steel and full granite kitchen with a dishwasher. On the ROOF DECK includes a beautiful skyline view of downtown and beyond, a SPA, plunge POOL. On the basement floor you will find a GYM including sauna and ping-pong table. Building includes 24 hr. SECURITY in lobby. On GROUND floor within a 1-block radius are several very popular CAFES and bars, including the 24/7 LA cafe, juice bar, salon, and hookah smoke lounge. Within a block are some of the best downtown restaurants, wine and beer shops, cafes and cocktail BARS. Apartment is professionally CLEANED for each guest. Clean, linens, towels, complimentary soap and provided for every stay. PARKING: Access to FREE parking in a lot minutes away. From apt it's a 20 min drive to West Hollywood/Beverly Hills, 20 min drive to Santa Monica/Venice Beach, 5 min drive (20 min walk) to Staples Center/LA Live/Convention Center. Within 2 blocks at Pershing Square is the red/purple subway line with access to Union Station and Hollywood and connecting lines to Pasadena, Santa Monica and Venice Beach and blue line access to the Convention Center/LA Live. This is a pretty spacious loft so its good for a single person who likes lots of space, but also roomy enough to fit up to four people. If you have any other questions about staying here I am more thank happy to answer them for you. Just want to make sure you have an amazing experience here. I look forward to having you!

                      <div data-reactid="1748">
                       1000 Square foot 1 bedroom loft on the 11th Floor in Historic Downtown Los Angeles. Doorman Secured Building. Fantastic city and mountain views from Balcony. Walking distance to great restaurants, bars, shopping, great nightlife literally steps away, LA Live and the Staples Center a short 15 minute walk. 55" Flat panel television(s) with Blu Ray Player(s) in Living room and Bedroom. WiFi. Sorry no Cable (Local channels only, you're in LA, why spend your time indoors watching television?) Beautiful Travertine floors throughout. Soaking Tub in Bathroom, Granite countertops. Weekly Maid Service, Roof Top Gym, Pool and Jacuzzi Subway is 2blocks away, hop on the train and be in Hollywood in 15 minutes, Universal Studios In 20 minutes. If you are visiting LA on the second week of the month you get to be apart of ArtWalk. The free, self-guided, public art phenomenon known as The Downtown Art Walk brings together art lovers and community friends to the ever evolving downtown Los Angeles. With exciting and unique offerings around every corner, downtown celebrates the arts each and every month on the 2nd Thursday. Many of The Downtown Art Walk activities take shape in and around the galleries predominantly on Spring and Main streets between 2nd and 9th streets. However, there is a plethora of art related events and openings, activities, and special programming that take place all over downtown. Welcome to my downtown.
                      </div>

                      <div data-reactid="2067">
                       <li data-reactid="2068"><p data-reactid="2069">The space was generally basic and fine and as pictured. It's a loft, so lighting isn't ample as is often the case with lofts. My main problem, however, was that a small cute rabbit lives in a cage in this apartment, and that information was not in the apartment description/information when I booked the space online. I would have liked to have known this when I booked- I had no notice of this fact until I checked in to the apartment. Other listings that I've seen detail that a pet lives in the space or will be sharing the space with you. The rabbit cage is an open grated cage and it's in the corner of a decent-sized studio with windows that face in towards the courtyard. When I first got there, it was sort of implied that the rabbit was going to stay with me in the apartment, although Vanessa may have offered to take the rabbit away with her- I can't remember. I was initially fine with the rabbit staying because I do love animals and it's a cute little thing. But I have always had cats and/or dogs as pets, and I don't know rabbits and rabbit maintenance as well. About halfway through my four-night stay, I started feeling uncomfortable that rabbit poop was accumulating in an open cage (that also has hay and other rabbit amenities) in a studio for a long period of time. I asked Vanessa if she could come by to clean up the poop, but ultimately we were unable to connect. Overall, the fact that a rabbit lives in the apartment should have been posted in the online ad so that people have notice of this fact. It's a cute little rabbit, but I would have liked to have known about this pet before booking. </p><span data-reactid="2070">Doug </span><span data-reactid="2071">2016-09-16T00:00:00Z</span></li>
